申報本埠增刊　業餘周刊特寫歌聲激昂中萬人痛哭聶耳先生  愛娥女士　　這位劃時代的作曲家—聶耳先生，今年才祗是一個二十四歲的靑年；在他的事業正當方興未艾的邁進中，竟出乎一般意想之外的會給太平洋的巨浪呑沒了，這難怪他的一般友人和愛聽他所作的樂曲的　衆，都懷着一顆破碎的心冒暑跑到金城戲院去傷感的追悼他呢！　　開追悼會的那天（星期五）早上，照例大部份的人都應該忙於他的職業，沒有工夫去追悼這位與自己並不相關的死者；然而事情是常會出於意外的，也正像他的死。這天早晨八點鐘以前，　集於金城門口的會衆，就把北京路的交通一部份斷絕了；三道頭和巡捕，忙着維持秩序，驅遂閒人，可是依舊沒有方法把這條交通孔道淸理出來。　　「爲啥還不開門哩？」性急的小姐望着鐵柵欄自言自語的說着。　　「九點鐘到快了罷？」另一個接着無目的的問。　　正在大家耳語得最起勁的當兒，幾扇紅心黑框的邊鬥突然開了，會衆就像一羣脫了竊勒的馬似的瘋狂的朝裏面衝着；同時砰隆砰隆的聲響鬧成了一片，連對面說話都聽不淸晰。這麼嘈雜的空氣一直延長到一刻鐘以上，大家才像有點感到累了似的慢慢平靜下去；可是，不時還有着一兩陣爲了爭座位而起的高潮。　　會塲裏並沒有什麼特別的佈置；台上祇掛着一幅很長的黑布的橫披，上書「上海各界追悼劃時代的作者聶耳先生」這幾個大字，和一張圍着花圈的遺像，此外便都是各團體和私人致獻的花圈；這在一些祇是爲着熱鬧而來的會衆，也許會感到大大的失望的。　　「佈置得這麼簡單！連輓聯也沒有！」好像是一個智識階級的靑年嘆息似的說着。　　「人可不少啊！」同伴中間一個穿長衫的中年人感到滿足似的不贊成那個靑年的批評。　　一會兒，電通的畫報在『人手一編」的被欣賞着，嘈雜的聲音便像熱度給冷氣衝散似的漸漸消沉了，連呼吸也彷彿成了聲響。可是不久，這靜寂如水的空間又從大門口漸漸動蕩起來，一直傳染到台口的會衆；大家都敏感的側着身朝後面看着，幾千隻眼睛好像白熱燈似的都照到了王瑩小姐的身上。　　「這個便是王瑩囉！」王瑩的出現又成了談話的中心了。　　可是，王榮還沒有坐下來，接着在前台右邊門口胡萍小姐又出現了，一般人又瘋狂似的把眼光一直送到她坐下以後才像感到吃力似的收了回來。　　胡萍這天穿着一件花旗袍，外罩着黑披肩，悲哀的情緒若隱若現的在臉上蕩漾着，熊度顯得異樣的沉靜；她在周劍雲隔壁的座位上坐了，眼睛不時的望着台上聶耳的遺像，似有無限的哀思。　　開會的時間愈逼愈近了，會衆又陸續到來了不少。有二千多個座位的金城戲院，這時也擠得水洩不通起來，上下　道上都挿滿了像地樁似的人，同時電通的趙邦　，周伯動—會塲幹事—兩個人忙得和演戲一樣前後跑着，嘴裏拉畏了聲音向會衆下着警告：「請樓上樓下的諸君坐下，這樣子下去是有危險的！」可是，即使這種於自己生命有關的警吿，也還是不能把他們那種熱烈的情緒按捺下去，似乎大家都抱了一種以身殉聶耳的心情來參加追悼似的；周伯動的話還沒說完，樓上太平扶梯上的門又像水衝破了堤似的湧進了二百多人，最後經了十多個人的努力才把這人的潮堵住了。　　也許是由於會衆熱烈的情緒表現得太過了吧，電通的攝影師和燈光管理員這時急急忙忙地把燈光和攝影機配置起來；到宣吿開會時，已經是九點一刻了。第一個走上去報吿的，是曾經和聶耳合作不少的歌曲的孫師毅君，這是電影界中一位靑年前進的劇作者。他在雷嗚似的鼓掌聲中，拉着哽咽的聲調簡略地報吿了一段聶耳死後的情形：「……我們發起這個追悼會，不是爲了單純的友情。我們爲的他是中國一位劃時代的樂曲作者，是一位能刻苦自勵的上進的靑年。他沒有進過音樂專門學院，也沒有浪費過他的時間；如果在音樂上有什麼成就的話，那什麼都是他自己在短促的二十四歲生涯中一點一滴獲取來的！他死後沒有什麽遺產，就是有的話，也不過是在百代有五張唱片和勝利兩張唱片可以收點版稅，某影片公司欠他一百多元，此外，那就祗有他一生心血結品的三十多個歌曲遺留下來……」他說到後來差不多要吐不淸字了；胡萍的眼淚往下淌着；會衆都拉長了面孔凝視着豪上，空氣凄凉得像一座古堡一樣。　　接着吿訴我們關於聶耳一生歷史的是雲南同鄉會鄭雨笙君，他說：「聶耳是生長在雲南的玉溪，原名守信，後來加入聯華，同事的因他的姓耳字多，大家都呌他一聶耳子」，他就索興改名聶耳了。他父親是一位很能吃苦的草藥醫生，靠一些土方法治愈了不少的病人，所以還有點小小的名氣。後來他想進一步的謀點發展，才把玉溪的醫窒搬到昆明；從老板，醫生，至店夥，學徒的事差不多都是他一手料理，有時聶耳的母親也相帮一下。這時，聶耳正在雲南聯合中學讀書，同一個女子中學的校長戀得火一般的熱烈，對於家事簡直不大過問。但甜密的學校生活還過不到二年，他便遭受了父親之死的打擊。他想往外省找尋他的生活蹊徑，可是他家裏的經濟狀况，在父親死後是更不能允許他的要求。這時恰巧遇某軍在雲南招收學生軍，於是他便乘這機會拋棄了愛人家鄕去過那軍人的生活。經過了三個月的時間，跟着軍隊在廣東，廣西，湖南，湖北，南京，上海都留過足跡；後來因爲他過不慣這種流浪的生活，便又重行回到故鄕。第二次的出門是帮助他哥哥到上海辦轉運事務所，他做了這所的主任。可是不久，他哥哥經營的商業停頓下來，他才投入明月歌舞社服務，但因與黎鋁暉君的思想大相徑庭，不久又脫離了明月社而進聯華第一廠，此後，才算有了讓他努力的機會。在聯華任事一年，月薪祇有卅元，以二十元維持生活，其餘的錢他還要用來做很多的事；他每月都要買點關於音樂的書籍，另外還請了一個俄國人敎曲。他對於音樂是那樣猛進的學習着，所以不等到離開聯華便給百代公司邀去擔任組織國樂團，使國樂有了新的使用。在百代的收入每月有百餘元，但他的生活還是和先前一樣的菲薄。這樣過了一年以後，又由百代轉入聯華第二廠服務，月薪從卅元增加到一百多元；在這時期中成就的有「大路』，「開路先鋒」等許多作品。但他不因此感到滿足，他對於音樂好像心裏有一個永遠塡不平的慾壑，所以在不久以前，便靠着歷年積下來的一點錢去到日本學習他所要學的一切更高深的藝術。他臨行時是那麼歡忻與自慰，連我們也爲着他歡忻而歡圻了；可是，時隔不久，我們却沒有想到我們暫時的分離會一變而爲永訣的……」聽衆像觸電似的，聽了這段血淚的訴說，都顯出一副灰黯的臉孔；白熱燈照在各人臉上像表演一幕影戲那麽的緊張。　　等到呂驥君上台報吿聶耳創作的生活時，台下又是一陣鼓掌聲。但呂君的臉色和說活的聲音已經是像剛剛放聲痛哭

過似的，他祇簡略的說了幾句：「關於聶耳先生的生平，剛才鄭先生說得很淸楚；我現在祇就他的創作生活來報吿一點，也許是可以做我們的模範的。他在譜「大路」和「開路先鋒時，爲了要使聲調能充分表現出各種不同的情緒，他曾經有一星期的時間成天的在馬路上走着，默察勞苦大衆的生活形態；晚上回去也是不住的哼着，像發了狂一般。因爲「開路先鋒」前面有幾個的爆炸聲，然而又是含着勝利的笑聲；他爲了要運用聲調表達出這種含意，就成天到晚都這麼「哈哈哈哈」地吃醉酒似的演習。他寓所的二房東常常在深夜聽到他這種笑聲，還以爲他是發了狂，第二天便忍不住跑上樓向他問了，才曉得他是在那裏練習歌曲……」他說得聲帶像斷了一樣，下面的話只是在喉　裏旋轉着；會衆的喧鬧也跟着他的聲調往下低沉，大家都被偉大的生活經歷的畫描攝取着，不再像先前祗當聽故事那麽單純的感情衝動了。　　「聶耳是死了，但他的遺音却仍値得我們的記億；現在要播送的就是他自己歌唱的「揚子江暴風雨」裏面幾隻歌曲：「開　」「苦力」「碼頭工人」「打磚」「打樁」。孫君重行上豪這樣報吿以後，　　又捲起了一陣高潮。　　聶耳的遺音播送完了，接着就是他遺作的演奏。再以後是「帵歌獨唱」，那是電通的演員王素賣力的演出；她爲了追悼聶耳，曾經費了較長的時間才練熟了這隻帵歌的。另外還有金燄的「再會吧，南洋！」王人美的「梅娘曲」，袁牧之，陳波兒合唱的「畢業歌」；但因為這幾個人中間有的不在上海，便用百代唱片來播送了。　　從九點鐘直到十二點鐘，會衆還是那麽整齊的不肯離開座位，可是我坐在那裏却像給什麽壓得吐不過氣來似的，心裏老是感着一種說不出的酸楚的滋味！訓練與修養自信與信人  行健　　處事做人都是很難的。別的不說，單就自信和信賴別人這一件事來說，就是如此。如果一個人捨己從人的，卽不自信而專於信人時，那麽你就會獲得一種盲從附和，受人播弄，缺乏自信心的譏評。反之，如果一個人是自有主張和定見的，或不輕於相信別人而具有自信的精神和魄力，那麽你就會獲得一種剛愎自用，自大自專的譏評。所以說處事做人是很難的，特別是在許多有矛盾性的事態中更易使人徬徨無主。　　但是，在另一方面，世俗的見解常常又只愛好偏執，對於任何事態都只喜歡下一個絕對的是或否的判斷，却反對人們把握一切事態的對立性，從對立中去認識眞理。比如就拿自信與信賴別人的事體來說，許多人就在這上面成爲絕對的機械論者，不是說絕對應該自信就是說絕對應該信人，這中間似乎沒讓你隨不同的情形而有任何取捨的餘。這種絕對論，機械論，獨斷論的觀別表現於現今的動盪的時代中。比如關於自信的問題；有許多人以爲各個人的意志和精神應該絕對地獨立自由，不受任何人的牽制和修改；自己的意志不但應該獨立，而且自己要有支配一切的偉大精神。這就是說人應該完全自信，不要信任別人。又有許多人以爲個人不應自信，應該絕對服從別人，完全受別人的領導，說保留個人的獨立精神和意志，這是絕對違反集體的精神的。這就是說，人應該絕對信賴別人，服從別人，不要有自信心。　　雖然這兩種俗見是絕對相反的，但又有許多人却在某種立場上將它們溶合爲一而表現爲絕對個人主義和專制主義，主張特定的少數人應有絕對的自由，主張他們的意志應當支配一切。因爲在他們想來，只有他們自己是應該保持其絕對的自由，其主張和見解不受任何評議與修正，應毫無顧慮地執行下去，所以這是絕對個人主義的。對於大衆呢？他們便是叫別人要絕對信賴自己，不許別人有絲毫的自信力，以便絕對服從自己，所以這是絕對專制主義的。這兩種俗見，兩種偏執的主張，完全是以自己個人的利益爲出發點，抹殺了社會的和衆人的利益與要求的處世哲學。這樣的處世哲學，目前是廣泛地流行於許多專制主義所支持的社會和民族中，事實非常顯然，但不管怎樣，這種處世哲學是有害於社會和大衆的，不能算是合理的處世哲學。　　正確的處世態度應當是每一個人也要能自信也要能信人，應不同的環境和條件去决定取捨，並且這種條件應該從社會與個人的利益兼顧中去看取，不應專以個人利益爲前提。假使我們自己的主張對於個人和社會確是有利益的，我爲了對自己和社會負責之故，應當不屈不撓地堅持到底，絕不捨己從人，就是說我要爲那正確的主張奮鬥到底，要有自信的毅力和担當的勇氣。反之，如果我們的主張縱然有利於自己個人，然而確實是有害於社會，有害於多數人，那麽這時我們就絕對不能剛愎自用，而應該信賴別人，應該接受別人的更正確的主張，修正自己的主張。因爲自信和信人都不能憑主觀的感情和利益來决定，所以自信不能因此就　　　　　　　　乃至專制的道路上去，而信人也不能因此就走上全無骨格，無定見，乃至盲從逢迎的道路上去。　　不但如此，而且在立足於以社會和自己的利益兼顧的條件下，立足於正確的處世哲學的原則下來談自信與信人，也一定要能自信的人才眞能信人，能信人的人才眞能自信；信人要以自信爲基礎，自信亦要以能信人爲基礎。因爲自信與信人都得要有正確的定見，那麽在自信時應該懂得自己所信賴的主張亦是別人所要求和相信的。我們要相信大多數人所要求和信賴的是正當的，然後自己也才敢相信自己的主張是正確的，才可以自信。如果我們完全抹殺了社會的要求，不相信社會上多數人的要求是正當的，只主觀地說自己的主張對，則終於不能有堅持自己的主張到永遠的勇氣，是不會發生堅强的自信心的。反之，如果我們完全沒有自己的觀察和意見，不知道審核別人的主張是否正確而只盲目地附和，就是自己也沒有相信那種主張之自信心，則這種信人也是不能堅定的，今天可以跟隨這個人跑，明天又可以跟隨那個人跑，社會上這樣的現象多得很。所以說要能自信的人才能眞信人，信人要以自信爲條件；要能信人的人才能眞自信，自信也要以能信人爲條件。　　我們常聽到說社會上應該有頒袖和應該信賴領袖，但怎樣作一個領袖和怎樣信賴我們的領袖，都必須懂得上述的一切。因爲一個領袖不是就應該把自己的主張認爲是絕對的，不顧社會的多數人的意志，甚至不讓多數人有意志而應絕對服從自己。如果是這樣，那便只是剛愎的自信，是沒有信賴社會和衆人的要求的基礎的自信。在信賴領袖時，也不是絕對的盲從，我們要能正確地審度了他的主張之後，認爲和自己的信念相符合，才能去信仰他。否則他的主張錯　時也只是信賴，那麼自己是對自己和社會不負責任，是沒有自信基礎的信賴別人。所有這樣的自信和信人，都不能算是正當的。因爲如果這樣，那領袖與羣衆的結合便不會堅實，羣衆對於領袖的信賴絕不是眞實的愛戴，領袖對於盡衆的領導也不是眞正的領導，從專制主義的內包中會潛伏着距心力的暗長，社會的隱憂就在那裏。星期文學會評「金瓶梅」  華生　　金瓶梅一書雖多述之於人們之口，但以久懸例禁，不許刋行，致毁譽參半，極少定評。這眞是一劍可惜的事情。　　是書作者世或傳爲明儒王元美所作，究否確實，尙須待諸考訂。然斷定其爲明代作品則似乎當無疑問。這僅是附帶說的幾句話，對於本文宏旨無甚關係，姑且放開不談，來專一說說這書的內容吧！　　如果說是紅樓夢主要的是正面描寫王侯宰相富有大家庭中的私生活，說明其安閒舒適的優游度日，則金瓶梅正是在反面的叙述一個勢豪之一生經歷，暴露其無惡不作。因之我以爲這兩本書，應該作爲姊妹篇，等量齊觀的一樣看待。何况這兩本書又恰是各自反映到當時社會一般普遍的情况呢！　　金瓶梅一書，雖主幹人物爲西門慶與潘金蓮，然由這兩個怪物所牽涉到的事物，則上自權奸之賣官　爵，下及奴婢之貪贓受賄，旁及社會人情之奸險欺詐，而處處無不以一個「財」字貫串其間，眞是　　　少有的一部大著作。如在書中開首第一回中便道：「…酒色財氣四件中，惟有財色二字更爲利害。這財色二字中，財字便更甚於色。怎見得財的利害？假如一個人，在那窮苦的田　，受盡無限凄凉，耐盡無端懊惱；晚來摸一摸米盟苦無隔宿炊糧；早起看一看廚前，愧沒半星烟火；妻子飢寒，一身凍餒；就是那粥飯尙且艱難，那有餘錢沽酒。……到那有錢的時候，揮金買笑，一擲巨萬，姬妾滿堂，也很容易。思飲酒眞個瓊漿玉液，不數那琥珀杯流；要鬥氣錢可通神，果然頤指氣使。趨炎的壓脊挨背；附勢的吮　舐痔。眞所謂「得勢疊肩事，失勢掉擘去」，古今炎凉世態，莫有甚於此者。」從這一段話看來，卽可知這本書的構成，不管其用那種事物來作爲對象，然其主要立足點，或者竟說牠唯一的立塲，則全以「財字—經濟爲基礎的去說明一切現象，而絕非如用一些玄妙的觀念所幻想出來的可比。　　西門慶本是一個商人子弟，因富有家私，便能上通官府，直達宰相之門，下結土棍，魚肉鄕民；這樣的便形成了官僚，商人，土豪等三位一體的壓迫勢力。這正是對有明中葉的一幅鮮明圖解。所以我們　到這本書，不只可以去意識到當時的社會機構，　且還可作爲官塲現形記，商人土豪劣紳史去讀。這本書唯其對於這些人特別描寫得深刻，所以觸犯了一般大老官的忌諱，便硬說是一些淫穢之言而懸爲例禁了。　　此外，關於本書描寫的技術，也是不讓於紅樓夢，水滸的。在這等地方，袁枚於原本金瓶梅跋中說得最清楚：「書中所紀，爲一勢豪之一生經歷，其所述事端以涉及婦女者爲最多。旁及權姦恣肆，朝政不綱，亦皆　事比附，隱加誅伐。而　園諧謔，市井俚詞，鄙　之言，殊異之俗，乃能收諸筆下，載諸篇章，口吻逼眞，維妙維肖，纔一讀及，便覺紙上躍然。作者多才多藝，有非傖俗所可幾及。才人文筆不同凡響，信乎人之欽企弗衰也。」所以我說這書不特應與紅樓夢爲姊妹篇去讀，堪當社會史去看，且更可當作爲文學書去一樣涉獵的。

大上海風光大滬花園之夜  史用　　上海這地方，一切都市的矛盾，都像木刻畫一樣的用粗綫條描畫在這一幅都市生活的模型上，深刻的，諷刺地。　　夏天啦，天上有赤烈的火傘髙罩着；地上有推着滿載笨重的鋼條的老虎車，踽踽地踏着滾然的柏油路的小工，有躱在咖啡館嚼着巧克力冰淇淋的姑娘少爺，也有索與躱到莫干山的山巓，靑島的海濱去的老爺太太。這里是窮人　貴人的分界，下等人類與上等人類的鴻溝！　　夜里，小菜塲及冷僻馬路人行道的水門汀上，苦力們在草　上做着呼呼的甜夢了，我們的老爺少爺太太奶奶和姑娘們也要去追求現實的甜夢了。　　露天電影塲上，人頭洶湧着，夜花園里，對對雙雙，鶯鶯燕燕，一　濃重的脂粉氣環繞着挺直的自嘩　西裝。他們和她們沒有夜，在都市裏，時鐘敲了十一句　，才是髙貴的男女們生命活　的時候。　　滬西，大滬花園也是都市男女的消魂地。　　這是帶着鄉村風味的僻靜所在，和市聲隔絕得很遠了。剛走　門口的時候，心頭感到這是一塊冷地了，可是你要是深入那核心中去，你會感覺到那確是一個比火球邊熱的火山啊！　　十點飾時候，夜花園里雖然火炬通明，光頭雲霄，但遊人還是疏疏落落的。草坪上陳滿了檯椅，喝汽水的却不多。賣女人用的脂粉香水的地方和利用機器作賭傳遊戲的地方，都有妖嬈的女人管　着，她們會不吝惜的投你一個勾魂的媚眼。熱心的人為了這一點享受，就將一個雙角銀毫投進那賭具的小口中去，旋轉復旋轉，玻璃箱里便有一個起　機似的東西落在箱底糖果啊假珠啊皮夾啊的面上，由是再旋轉再旋轉，好！鈎住了珠子了，旋轉旋轉，……呀！旁觀的一羣人都叫起來了。但珠子仍然落在箱底里。撲的，又一個雙角銀亳投進去，又是旋轉旋轉冉旋轉，鈎住了，鈎住了，留神，穩鈎住了！　的——喲！又落在箱底了！『　的，老子不信，再來。」於是又一個雙毫投進了小口，那年輕人並不因失敗而灰心，他是富於堅忍心的，他投入的雙毫早巳超過購買琥珀色假珠的代價了，但是他依然聚精會神地努力着，額頭，鼻尖，滿是汗珠，玳瑁眼鏡也落在鼻尖上。雖然結果還是鈎不到珠子，但他終於從那管理賭具的小女郞處領受到一個會心的微笑了。　　桌上髙而夫的生意頗冷淡，因那個巳不如這新玩意兒的能够吸引人了。　　立在九曲橋上俯視池而，銀光點點，絢爛奪目，遊艇在　　穿梭，情侶們正興奮着呢　　站在這里聆西邊舞廳中傳來的樂聲，那粗俗的桃花江正震蕩着。　　火山上——舞廳里，坐檯子的也像月夜的疏星，陰森森地。樂聲一起，除少數舞客上火山外，勉應市面的只是舞女與舞女自己互摟着踏着緩慢的狐步罷了。　　據說大滬的市面還是挺興盛的呢！大概因為時候還早着的緣故。確實，不久舞廳里的人頭漸漸多了，人氣也漸漸旺了。樂師們的蘇哪，梵珴玲也似精神百倍了，樂聲剛剛停止，第二次的樂聲又接着響了，舞女們幾乎連略一坐定的機會也沒有。　　黯淡的燈光下面，一雙雙像浮萍在水浪中似的溒過去，西裝，長衫，短袖，蟬翼長袍，交文的內衣　，油　，粉　，　　，肉，腿，……成一片。　　「猴急」的舞客，將舞女抱了個滿懷，樓得幾乎要將她藏到衣袋里去似的。然而那舞女確也頗能體諒那舞客的一片用心，將髙聳的乳峯頂住男人的胸懷，滿頭飄散的髮浪斜傾在那男人的肩頭，將帶着蕩意的眼光斜晚着，男人聞着輕綃里透出來的陣陣肉香，心頭的鹿撞擊着，整個的沈醉了，樂聲也瘋狂的急遽的顫動着，火山眞要爆裂了。　　都市里什麽都新奇的：男人會找舞女跳舞，女人也一樣會找舞女跳舞。一位黑紗長袍的漂　少女也找了一個舞女在火山裏　轉着。可不知道她也同樣能感到肉的滿足嗎？　　檯子旁起了會話。　　——萬走吧？　　——呸，不要阿木林，梁賽珍還沒來呢！　　草坪中的音樂亭裏，這時也在奏樂了：可可咚咚，絃　齊鳴了，聲音幽　而略帶凄凉，似不與這世界相調和。　　都市的葬曲啊！　　草坪上的遊人，漸漸都圍攏來，小孩們更是髙興的奔實着。　　——跳水了！哈！　　——哈，一男一女，看！跳水了！　　頭都獃向那髙塔似的長梯。這又是都市裏的新刺激。　　兩個西洋人：男的穿着紅色的游泳衣，女的穿着白色的游泳衣，猴子似的爬上長梯，向觀衆行了一個禮，爬上去，爬上去，紅衣的爬上頂端，白衣的在下一層，望上去足足有五六丈髙。女的站上跳板，忽的，兩手向前空一擺，上身前俯，身子巳在半空里了，咚——，那白衣女人跌入長梯前的一個直徑不滿一丈的小圓缸裏了！漲水四濺，觀看的人不由得透了一口氣，髙聲呼叫了！　　接着紅衣人在梯頂的跳板上做了個更優美的跳水姿勢，兩脚豎立着，人在半空裏像幼時玩的一隻竹蜻蜓似的落下來　　——還有呢？跳火呢！　　——看啊，看跳火！　　那兩個人帶着火種，仍舊爬上長梯去。人們的情緖更加興奮了。缸裏水面上也裝着搿司林。鼻孔里充滿了搿司林的氣息。　　那女人唧嚦嚦的與上層的男子交換了幾句話後，便燃着火種。火在背上熊熊的燒着，火光從空中撲下，跌在缸里，滿缸都是火了。那男的在這萬分緊張的空氣里也燃着火種，從髙梯上跳下來，人跳在滿缸的火裏，缸里的水一被激動，水浪四　，火便完全熄了！　　這底是文明的游戲呢？原始的魔術呢？　　歸途中，對這絢　的都市又多了一層認識了。介紹「新文字月刋」　　上海中文拉丁化研究會編印之「中國話寫法拉丁化——理論。原則。方案』一書，出版以來，備受讀者歡迎，於出書後兩個月中初版卽吿售罄。現聞該書增訂第二版，巳於日前出書，內容較初版更為完備，而定價仍為二角五分。又該會最近創刋「新文字」（Sin　Wenz）月刋一種，第一期巳於八月十五日出版。內容有新文字理論，寫法討論，消息，及各種新文字讀物，詩歌等等，頗為豐富。該刋另售每期三分，預定全年三角五分。以上兩種書報，本埠各大書店及四川路底內山書店均有代售。徵求郵票及畫刋　　茲欲徵求新疆四川雲南賭省郵票及申報圖畫特刋第九十三期至九十六期各一份，願割讓者請於每日下午五時至七時駕臨寗波路四七六號華成烟草公司與余廉泉君接洽，酬報從豐。海外通訊網黑人國總動員  耀光　　阿比西尼亞京城通訊　　隨着意阿衝突之發展，阿比西尼亞之名已為世人所大大地注意了。但是，這個國家的一切情形，却不是任何善於想像的人所能想像得到的。首先，阿比西尼亞是在非洲的熱帶地，若依當識判斷，這當然是一個荒涼酷熱的國家，但是，出你意料之外，阿比西尼亞却是一個美好的山國。這兒氣候是很溫和的，幾乎四季皆春，這兒的自然風景也很綺麗，所謂「阿此西尼亞」這個名稱，就有天上樂土的意味。至於國民，當然是黑色人種，但是，世界其他各地的黑人是沒有自己的國家的，所以阿比西尼亞要算是世界唯一的黑人國了。雖然因為牠的經濟，文化落後，在實際上是受着英法意等國的控制，但在名義義上牠却是一個獨立的帝國，因此牠還保有其存在意義，尤其是對於黑人。　　阿比西尼亞這個國家是何時建立起來的，考古家和歷史家們沒有一致的判斷；有的說是在紀元前五千年，有的則說是在紀元前五千八百年。但是，牠興被稱為文明古國的埃及在古代就有往還，這是巳經證明了的。依英國某著名考古學者的考察，在埃及繁榮時代的英主茨塔加美的　廟中曾記錄着埃及與阿比西尼亞往來之事；同時，據說以前伊斯來人，因被埃及壓迫，曾相率逃往地中海東岸，其中有一隊與其本隊分離了，後來到了風光明媚的高原地帶，找得了棲息之所，卽現今之阿此西尼亞。由此可見阿比西尼亞確是有很古的歷史的。　　然而，最使人驚奇的，乃是這個國家在過去三千餘年的歷史中都是被同一系統的皇室所統制的，現在阿比西尼亞的皇帝已是二百五十代的皇帝了。這種情形，恐怕是任何國家所沒有的吧，但不管你是否相信，事實却是如此的。依這里的一般的傳說，在紀元前一千年之際，在地中海沿岸有燦爛的文化足以誇耀者乃是猶太，其國王名梭羅門，聽到當時作為西巴的女王而被知道的阿比西尼亞女王瑪格達是具有沈魚落雁之容的絕世美人，乃遣使促之入宮，同時，女王亦早慕梭羅門王的英名，憧憬猶太文化，因卽應召幸王的宮殿。於是不久卽產生了黑色的皇太子。這便是現今阿比西尼王的祖先。此事就在舊約全書上也略有記載，想來當不致是毫無根據的傳說罷。　　關於瑪格達女王所生的皇太子建立其阿比西尼亞帝國的事情，此間還有一些奇怪的傳說。據云這個皇太子在梭羅門王處受敎育，於十八歲時卽具有文武全才，於是他卽從十二個村子里各集合了一千猶太人，率領歸返母國。但當其臨行時携走了國書，事為　羅門知道了　　以下接第五版

，在其大驚失色之下，即刻就派兵追捕皇子；當皇子從間道跑至紅海岸時，無法前進，而後面追兵又到，正在危急萬分之際，忽然大地崩裂，現出了一條到阿比西尼亞去的大道，於是皇子乃得越紅海而至土地肥沃具有天險的基格勒高原，定都亞庚沙母，建立了他的阿比西尼亞帝國，一直存在到而今。至於追趕皇子的追兵，後來因崩裂的大她復合，都被活埋在土中了。這樣的傳說當然是很神秘的，但阿比西尼亞之建國很古，和牠過去三千餘年以來都是爲同一系統的皇室所統制的事情，却是沒有疑問的。　　然而，阿比西尼亞之成爲現在這樣統一的帝國，乃是十九世紀之末的事情，這以前還是羣雄割據的局面。不過，就是現在，阿國雖在一個皇帝統制之下，但地方的封建勢力依然很大。國王在形式上是支配全國的，各地知事也歸國王任命，但事實上各地知事乃是世襲，國王的任命不過是一種形式罷了；而且各地知事都可任意擴充兵力。其與地方人民的關係完全是主僕的關係，他們握有對於人民的生殺予奪之權，而皇帝對於人民反沒有直接行使的什麽權力。這里流行的有這樣的一個諺語：『怎樣的犬，也不知道其主人的主人』。這便可以表明阿國皇帝與地方知事和其人民之關係的實情了。不過，在大體上，知事還是沒有反對皇帝的力量，還是要服從皇帝的命令，所以牠才能被稱爲統一的王國。　　因爲文化落後，阿比西尼亞人多半都是敬神信鬼的迷信家。無論家庭的禍福，個人的災難，乃至國家的興亡，他們都是求　　毛的。所以，在這里的巫師之類頗受歡迎，一般人若過有疾病災難，都要去求他們解救。不過，近年以來，阿國已在努力維新，如創辦學校，開設醫院，接受西方文化，都在積極進行中。　　阿比西尼亞旣是世界上唯一的黑人的獨立國家，其國民當然是極愛他們這個國家的。自華爾華爾事件發生，意阿一衝突開始以來，此間人士的愛國熱情卽日益高漲。他們雖沒有很多的飛機，坦克車，戰艦，他們雖缺乏現代的軍事利器，但他們却都具有一顆愛國的熱心，都抱着寗死也不作亡國奴的志願，以抗禦其强暴的敵人。在這里，無論是在街頭，在商店里，在家庭中，人們都在討論着意阿問題，都充滿了爲國抗敵的空氣。在這里，無論是王公貴族，或庶民百姓，都願爲國犧牲，跑到戰塲上去流盡其最後一點熱血。在這里，不僅是軍隊動員，而且全國國民也總動員了，一切都表現出了戰時的狀態。日前此間且有幾百貴族婦女舉行大示威，在阿國綠黃色國旗的飄蕩之下，表現出了牠們的愛國熱情。單就這點看來，也可想到目前阿國人民的情感是如何的激昻，戰爭空氣在這里是如何的濃厚了。　　現在，戰爭危機日益迫近，意國具有現代化之軍隊，各方面都較阿比西尼亞强得多，要戰敗落後的阿國，據情理說來，當然是很可能的；不過，以阿　人民現刻所表現出的愛國精神來說，意大利是否能征服他們，還是一個疑問；更何况東菲問題並非意阿兩國的簡單問題呢？專述華僑在全世界（八）  鍾民誼　　「目前政府對於馬來各州最注意的，便是發展錫　，以充主要的收入。但是華人在這裏的勢力不斷地發展，加以不斷地努力，向這佔世界錫的產額之半的市塲發展，因此，遂造成華人今日在馬來半島的地位。目前馬來政府與人民，雖極力運用法律的威力與聯合能力，亦不足以阻共勢力的進展。在白人丕寗　勒到馬來半島以前，華人便已在此從事鑛業，商業及漁業等。在初期中，一切道路之修造，公共事業之設置，以及各種統治之設施，基礎皆爲華人所手創；他們開關了許多荒地和山林爲耕地，冒各種危險，以獲取大的利益，同時又和酷烈的氣候奮鬥。他們一方面從事鑛山開採，同時又從事燒炭業，以供煉鑛之用，從事伐木，石匠，煉瓦等業，以供從事建築事業之用。便是政府的建設橋梁，鐵道，海港工程等偉大的建築事業，他們也祖任了大部分的工作。他們在國內各方面投資，從事各種商業。馬來與各港開定期航船的開始，也是華人。由此可知華人對於馬來的改造實　力不少，我們應予以同情和諒解。』　　華僑在馬來之地位於茲可見。　　馬來的生活程度很高，較上梅的也要高三倍。不過，在此間從事各種事業者的收入也很多，普通就是一個小商人或工人，每日亦可獲得純利二三元。所以，在此間的華僑有很多是富有的；卽是一般小商人和工人的生活也不很壞。　　不過，因爲馬來的政權操在英人之手，所以華僑的各種活動亦多感不便，許多地方都非受英人的支配不可；單以金融一項來說，在這裏雖有幾家資本　雄厚，信用昭著的華僑銀行，但在匯兌市價方面都是聽命於匯豐銀行的。　　同時，因爲此間華僑的生活優裕，在英人的懷柔政策之下，他們對於祖國也不很關心；特別是其中的「傌傌」（Babas—卽先期到此地的華人與馬來女人結婚所生的混血兒），他們沒有受過中國敎育，他們相信回敎，對於祖國的關心可以說絲亳沒有，甚至連中國話也不會說，自然也聽不懂。　　三　印度及港澳等地的華僑　　印度　　就廣義的南洋說來，印度本可歸入南洋之內。但因印度在遠東所處地位之重要，其與我國關係之深切，所以特在此將其單獨提出來談論。　　印度與中國同爲亞洲文明古國，中國與之發生關係當然很早。在漢晉時代兩　的往來就很密切了；及至唐代，這兩個文明古國的關係是更加密切，相傳玄莊赴印度取經的史實，便是這密切關係之事實的表現。　　但是，在宋元以前，我國的經濟還沒有大的發展，因而國民出國經營工商業，僑居海外者可說　沒有；過去中國人之往印度者只不過是爲的求法求道而已，所以沒有久居印度的僑民。及至海通以還，國民出國經營工商業或作工謀生者才日益增加，於是在印度才有了華僑的形影。　　印度華僑都是分住在加爾各答·加嶺崩與大吉嶺·孟買·　都拉斯·錫蘭等地的。就中以在加爾各答者爲最多，我們可以說加爾各答的華僑是印度華僑的代表。　　加爾各答是由東方海道入印度的門戶，是印度的第一大都會。在這裏共有華僑約萬人，其中以廣東人最多，福建人次之，湖北和山東人亦有。　　他們在這裏與在南徉各地的僑胞不同：南洋各地的僑胞是經營大工商業，動輒就有幾十萬幾百萬乃至幾千萬的資產；加爾各答的華僑呢？多半是做小工，生活窮苦，很少有富豪之家。生活窮苦者當然不能講漂亮，所以住在加爾各答的「支那衕」的華僑，各方面都是富於寒酸氣的；再加以中國國際地位的不如人，致使這些窮苦的僑胞到處受人輕視。（未完）播音節目特別節目　　紅光藝友社　　華東（一三六〇）上午九時至十時　　賣報歌（歐陽琦）戀愛明星（胡珊珊）特別快車（張莉）吹泡泡（杜琳蓮）大路（吳　）定情歌（全體）雲夜孤怨（陳美英）航空救國（閣　　李樹德（九四〇）下午六時至七時　　夜間嘯（前奏曲）夜來香（鄭霞）永遠親愛（莉亞）賣油條（蓓蓓）開路先鋒（佩洪主唱）永別了弟弟（鄭霞）風雨歸舟（莉亞）　花女（蓓蓓）畢業歌（全體）　　利利（一二四〇）下午六時半至七時半　　賣報歌（歐陽琦）航空救園（胡珊珊）特別快　（張莉）吹泡泡（杜琳蓮）雪夜孤怨（陳美英）明星（蘭心）大路（英驛）定情（全體）　　大上海社　　亞聲（一一二〇）上午九時半至十一時半　　淸早起來（琳琍）間仙子（飛亞）慈母搖籃曲（飛虹）戀愛明星（王瑛）四時吟（莫竇）關外高歌（琳琍）舟中曲（王瑛）戰臥沙塲（飛亞）梅花接老爺（飛虹）永遠親愛（莫　）船夫曲（琳琍）因爲你太美（飛亞）丁丁噹太太（飛虹）（莫竇）航空救國（王瑛）英雄夫婦（飛虹）　　中國兒童文化恊會　　新新（七八〇）中午十二時至一時　　（一）兒童歌唱新曲（二）徐紹昌先生故事（三）黃亦晨先生故事（四）張友鑑先生報告（五）華光口琴隊吹奏「昭君怨」「皇后」兩曲。　　晨鐘口琴隊　　華東（一三六〇）下午一時至二時　　石人望先生敎授（標準口琴吹奏法）（半音口琴）（手風琴）（口琴隊鋼璈大合奏）（大衆隊）野戰隊進行曲（德國著名司丹口琴隊唱片）愛底回憶（王康寗）卡門（劉逸）却來說夜總會（二重奏）（王康寗）（陳庭磚）平沙落雁（秦泰來）我不願伴舞（沈濂）La　cucaracba（高濬生）沙漠舞塲（三重奏）（劉逸）沈廉）（高濬生）　　國語會敎授蘇音　　佛音（九八〇）下午二時一刻至三時　　（一）講故事（分家）（二）敎蘇音課本（第二十四課）（三）唱歌（做好人上）（四）變戲法（巧變白米）　　中華口琴隊　　新新（七八〇）下午三時一刻至四時　　大軍進行曲（大合奏）普力瑛的船歌（短音階和音分解奏法）（王慶隆）探戈「羅刹」（獨奏）長想思（三重奏）（丘文章，曾凱超，蔣力鴻）夫人請讓我吻你的手（陳劍晨）巴城酋長序曲（二重奏）（王慶隆，柯耀宗）吹口笛的路夫斯（夏國範）西班牙進行曲（大合奏）（口琴隊）　　稚鳴社　　交通（一三〇〇）下午五時至六時　　小桃紅（前奏曲）甜蜜的夢（璐玲）漂泊者（陳萍）鳳求凰（兪徵）休息五分鐘（珂玲）愛情如玫瑰（柴瑟）春潮回來吧（陳萍）（斐君）夜花園裏（璐玲）賣花詞（斐虹）小鸚哥（莉玲）（王瑛）西宮詞（埃娜）桃李刦（全體）　　中華兒童故事播音社　　永生（一〇八〇）下午五時至五時半　　「鐵鞋兵」徐紹昌先生講　　總該有這麼一天罷？把人家壓迫得太厲害了，把人家愚弄得太過份了，雖然是馴伏慣的縣羊，雖然是自己　養的狗羣，也會咆哮怒吼的呀！也會叛亂譁變的呀！（本故事寓有深意，請聽衆細味內容）。　　時代說書播音社　　佛音（九八〇）下午五時至六時　　「娜拉」續上星期　　易十生的傑作「娜拉」，誰沒讀過，可是他的題材却是取自當日的新聞，那新聞是記戴着一位主婦爲了要佈置會客室，可却沒有錢，所以娘就把丈夫放在抽屜里的支票，簽了丈夫的名字去取欵，終於夫妻吵起。……　　兩路上北員工俱樂部平劇組　　永生（一〇八〇）下午九時起　　爲水災籌賬宣傳播音　　鄧心厂君（上天台）丁樹保君（太君辭朝）孫伯康君李世文君（四郎探母）孫仲賢君（托兆磁　）黃培明君（打鼓爲曹）黃麗生君丁義華君（別　）沈保年君（雙御園）林雅言君（武昭　）陳順孫君（捉放曹）馬　文君（六月雪）王健侯君（戰太平）張怡生君（空城計）沈詩義君（洪羊洞）張之讓君莊炳南君（汾河灣）蘇少　君（桑園寄子）電影消息鄭正秋先生追悼大會　　今日下午二時在瀾社舉行　　我國電影界先進明星影片公司協理鄭正秋先生，一生盡瘁影　，而其對於社會公衆事葉，努力尤多，自於七月十六日晨逝世，銀海星沉，舉國哀痛，且鄭氏生平，待人接物，可以肝　相照，凡有求者，尤爲慷慨好助，以是全國各界，更爲惋惜。茲有本市廣東旅滬同鄕會，明星影片公司，上海潮州會館，潮州旅滬同鄕會，中國文化建設恊會上海分會，中國敎育電影恊會上海分會，上海社會敎育社，上海潮惠會館，上海潮州和濟醫院，華威貿易公司，中央影戲公司，冠生園食品公司，上海市話劇研究會，恒社，新時代影片公司，民國中學校，上海粤僑商業聯合會，華豐織印綢廠，中央電影事業指導委員會，丁仲英醫室同人，無錫無錫大戲院，南京首都大戲院股份有限公司等三十餘　體，發起於今日下午二時假座湖社舉行鄭正秋先生追悼大會，以表哀悼，並誌紀念。其追悼節目如下：　　一·開會，二·奏迎賓樂，三·鳴鐘，四·起鼓，五·主祭團就位，六·同祭者就位，七·全體肅立，八·主祭團詣遺像前，九，奏哀樂，十·上香，十一·獻花，十二·讀祭章。十三·唱輓歌（明星公司全體演員），十四·靜默，十五·行禮，十六·家屬叩謝，十七·奏哀樂，十八·主席團復位，十九·同祭者復位，十二·致開會辭，二十一·報吿行述，二十二·演說，二十三·提案，二十四·家屬答辭，二十五·奏送賓樂，二十六，閉會。　　凡個人參加者，均須事前向法租界西自來火街昇平里潮州旅滬同鄉會領取參加證，臨時參加者，一律請回駕云。「自由神」觀後感  平野　　「自由神」是從「五四」一直到最近的革命運動的紀錄。在國產片中，還是一張僅有的有意義的歷史片。　　紀錄了這革命的歷史的段片之外，「自由神」的主題還吿訴了觀衆自由的門爭還不曾獲得勝利，被壓迫的人們應該靠自己的力量，去實現做一個「堂堂的人」　　所謂「一個堂堂的人，」當然是非常抽象的，可是，聰明的觀衆看那羣受壓迫的孩子這一塲面，多少能理解作者的思想了吧！　　假如「自由神」看作單純的描寫婦女解放的作品，那是錯誤的，王瑩飾演的這一女主角的生活描寫，不過是五四至「以後」的革命地程中的典型事件：五四運動推翻了封建勢力，解放了個人的自由，兩性問題婚姻的自由是足以代表新勢力抬頭的現象的。以後的上海事件的避免，當然是個疵點，可是很聰明地記下了廣州事件。北伐軍革命的描寫和戰士的生活的墮落，那也是很現實的。最後的新的轉變說明了這大時代的戰士們責任。所遺憾的，是對於軍閥戰事的描寫太不够了。　　不錯，一切都是藏頭露尾的，尙幸不曾歪曲了事實，在觀衆銳利的眼光之前還能明瞭片子的主題和它的思想。　　導演者司徒慧敏先生，是一個新的導演。在這裏，他多少運用了紀錄的手法來表現各個時期，所以後半部的片子顯得活潑。其他局部技術也很可觀。但是司徒先生對於演員的戲的支配許多地方顯得呆滯，有幾個塲面用很慢的調子企圖獲得效果，但是失敗了。　　演員中王瑩的戲也是半部較生動，前半部有許多地方顯得過失或呆滯，但較之她過去的作品是進步了；施超的戲不能儘量發揮，周伯動顧夢鶴均稱職，値得注意的是沒有幾個鏡頭的藍義，她留給了觀衆一個深刻的印象。　　佈景很可觀，攝影則未見特長。收音較之電通過去的作品也進步了。　　「由神」在演出上的確有失敗的地方，但大體上說來還可觀，而且這片子的內容是那麽有意義的自由的鬥爭的歷史的紀錄，是被壓迫者爭取自由的呼號，無論如何，這一片子是値得推薦給廣大的電影觀衆的。「自由神」主演者王瑩

1935.08.25

Continued Rise in Slight Floodwaters: Northern Jiangsu Disaster Area Expands; Weihu West Embankment Auxiliary Embankment Completed; Five Counties Along the Canal Strictly Guard Against Floods; Tongshan Establishes Yellow River Disaster Relief Association; Jiangsu Provincial Government Cables All Counties Under Xuzhou to Hasten Autumn Harvest 1

(Qingjiangpu) The Weihu Lake water level rose 24 centimeters yesterday and today. The lake mouth recorded 36.347 meters. Yaowan rose six inches, and Suqian rose two inches. The gangplanks of the boat bridges at the North and South gates of Qingjiang have been moved to the highest level of the stone steps. However, the water is not turbid. Xu Dingkang, the head of the canal area flood control office, has telegraphed the five counties along the canal again to prepare sacks, reed mats, and firewood, and to conscript laborers to avoid any negligence. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) The Yellow River water is still flowing down rapidly on the 24th. The Bulao River and Jing River have many obstructions, and the discharge is not smooth. The area of flooding is gradually expanding. Areas in the two river basins where embankments have not been built have all become disaster areas. North of Pipa Mountain, a vast expanse of water is seen. Residents of the disaster area who have not been able to escape are mostly taking refuge on rooftops. Firewood, grass, furniture are floating with the water. The severity of the disaster is no less than that in Western Shandong. All autumn crops, although some have matured, have been submerged because the villagers have been conscripted to build embankments and have not been able to harvest them. Disaster victims who have escaped find it difficult to survive, while those who have not escaped are trapped in their houses and trees like prisoners awaiting death. They desperately hope that outsiders will find ways to rescue them. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) The disaster area in northern Jiangsu has expanded. Disaster victims in Pei County are requesting the Special Commissioner's Office to issue passports to leave the area to avoid disaster. Shao Hanyuan, considering that it is not easy for disaster victims to leave, allocated 1,000 yuan to provide emergency relief to aid them. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) According to a Jinpu Railway report, the floodwaters of the Jing River reached Maocun Station yesterday. The shantytowns outside the station and nearby residents have gathered on the station platform to avoid the water. Fortunately, the roadbed is very solid and there has been no danger. The water level at Luozhuang Station is also high, and residents near the station are fleeing to avoid the disaster. Currently, traffic is not obstructed, but if the water continues to rise, it is feared that it will affect transportation. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) People from all walks of life in Tongshan established the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association at the county party headquarters today. They will immediately begin conducting investigations, raising funds, and providing relief. Lan Weibin and four others have been elected as standing committee members to oversee the operations. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) The auxiliary embankment on the west bank of Weihu Lake will be fully completed on the 24th. County Magistrate Wang returned to Xuzhou from the embankment construction site on the evening of the 24th. According to him, if the Yellow River floods continue to pour in and the water rushes down fiercely, all embankments may be ineffective. The Yellow River Prevention Association has decided to convene a meeting within days to discuss and plans only to defend the city and suburbs, and to stop conscripting people from the villages to build embankments, allowing them to quickly harvest autumn crops and prepare to flee. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) The Xuzhou authorities are still doing their utmost to prevent the Yellow River floods and desperately building embankments. The large embankment from Pipa Mountain to the Jinpu Railway section has been completed. From the 24th, another 3,000 villagers from the fifth and seventh districts were conscripted to build an auxiliary embankment on the south bank of the Bulao River from Pipa Mountain to Xiaoyangchang, a distance of eight li. At the same time, 2,000 laborers from the sixth district are building the southern section of the Bulao River embankment from the east of the Jinpu Railway to Jing Mountain. Because the embankments on both sides of the Jinpu Railway roadbed are facing a significant flood flow, fearing that the soil will be breached, 600 cubic meters of large stones allocated by the Jinpu Railway are being used to protect the embankment slopes on both ends, and the railway is responsible for filling the drainage ditches on both sides of the roadbed. All of this began on the 24th. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

(Zhenjiang) The Weihu embankment has breached, which will encroach on the central canal. The situation is critical. On the 24th, the water level reached 36.347 meters, close to the high water level of the fifteenth year of the Republic. The canal area is rushing to build the Bulao River embankment, ordering Si and Su counties to each conscript 5,000 laborers to assist. Pi County is building embankments and pre-organizing a team of strong men to protect the embankments, transport materials, and deal with emergencies. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) The Jiangsu Provincial Government, considering that the Yellow River floods are directly heading towards Weihu Lake and flooding northern Jiangsu, and although the counties of Xuzhou and Huai are defending, it is feared that human efforts will not be enough, has cabled all counties under Xuzhou to hasten the harvesting of autumn crops to ensure the people's food supply. Farmers in Tongshan districts, because they have been conscripted to build embankments, have no time to attend to agricultural affairs. Now, women and children are harvesting the crops. The people's strength is exhausted and their vitality is greatly damaged. When the Yellow River floods arrive, they may not even have time to escape. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 23rd)

(Qingjiangpu) The canal continues to rise, and the situation is quite dangerous. Yaowan rose nine inches, with a water depth of one zhang five chi nine cun. Suqian rose eight inches, with a water depth of one zhang four chi five cun. The river channel is full, and there is still a tendency to continue rising. If the Yellow River water from upstream flows south rapidly, the situation along the canal will be dire and unimaginable. According to a dispatch from Pei, Weihu Lake has risen another 16 centimeters. The canal area flood control office has ordered all counties along the canal to prepare materials for emergency repairs. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) According to a dispatch from Pei, the water level at Longguji rose one meter due to heavy rain in northern Pei County. Because it is rainwater and not Yellow River floods, the embankment is safe. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) According to a dispatch from Feng, there was a strong wind and rain in northern Feng County, and the northern embankment is in danger. They are rushing to protect the east branch of the Yi River embankment to protect the main embankment. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Xuzhou) The Shandong Provincial Construction Department telegraphed the Tongshan Special Commissioner's Office on the 23rd, stating that Shandong Province plans to build the east embankment of the canal in Xiazhen to the east, passing through eight li of Pei County. Construction has already begun within Sheng County. Please order Pei County to connect the construction and Pei County to immediately conscript laborers to work with Teng County to complete this embankment. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Qingjiangpu) Xu Dingkang, the director of canal flood control, took the Xin Chun special launch along the central canal to inspect the embankments northward on the morning of the 24th. It is said that he will go as far as Yaowan in Pixian County. One theory is that he is going to Yaosu to welcome Xu Kai, the chief engineer of the Huai River harnessing association, to discuss Yellow River flood prevention matters. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Zhenjiang) According to news from a certain Jiangsu water conservancy agency, the west embankment of Weihu Lake has collapsed, and water has entered Fengpei. The serious situation in northern Jiangsu may be alleviated, but the Yellow River flow is rapid and rising fiercely. On the 24th, the water level at Hanzhuang reached 38.3 meters. All water stations at Yaowan and Suqian have also increased, with no decrease. The future is truly worrying and we cannot be optimistic. Therefore, we have been strictly ordering all flood control areas and relevant county magistrates, day and night, to intensify the expansion, even if unfortunately the Yellow River water invades the south, we will never allow it to enter Hong Lake, and will not cause incalculable losses to the abandoned rivers. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Serious Disaster Situation in Eastern Hebei 2

(Tianjin) Due to the expansion of special forces in Eastern Hebei, farmland has been ruined. Recently, due to floods, refugees in the Funing Liushouying area are selling their children. Shi Lie, a counselor of the Political Reorganization Committee, and Secretaries Sun Baigang and Xin Tang are investigating the situation in the rural areas of the war zone. They arrived in Tangshan via Yutian on the evening of the 23rd and went to Funing County. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

South Canal Water Overflowing: Embankment Breached in Dexian County 3

(Tianjin) Three breaches have occurred in the earthen embankment at Huguanyingzi in Dexian County in the third section of the South Canal. The water is overflowing. More than 7,000 laborers have retreated to the old embankment. The current water level has risen to 25.37 meters. The low-lying embankments are in danger of collapsing. Thousands of laborers from Jingxian and Wuqiao counties are rushing to assist in the emergency repairs. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Tianjin) The South Canal Bureau received urgent telegrams from Jingxian and Wuqiao counties again on the 24th, stating that water is seeping through the Zhangjiaquan embankment on the west bank of the canal, for a length of about two li, and the situation is extremely dangerous. They are currently working together to repair the breach, but there is a shortage of wooden stakes, sacks, and lead wire. Please allocate them quickly for emergency use. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Sudden Rise in Yongding River Water Level 4

(Tianjin) The water level of the Yongding River at the Huilongmiao Lugouqiao reached nine and a half feet on the night of the 23rd, half a foot higher than the previous day. The current in the central channel of the new embankment is rapid, and the scouring force is quite strong. The River Bureau ordered the section chief to supervise the workers to defend the embankment on the 24th. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Heavy Rain in Shaanxi Province Washes Away the Ba River Embankment 5

(Xi'an) Shaanxi Province has experienced heavy rains for several days. Due to the downpour of mountain floods from Zhongnan Mountain, all rivers including the Wei River have risen. The newly repaired embankment of the Ba River has been washed away twice. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Police and Militia Cooperate to Block Bandits Outside the Pass 6

(Beiping) Yang Er, the leader of bandits both inside and outside the Great Wall in Xinglong, led more than 300 men, including more than 100 mounted bandits, fully armed. They arrived at Malan Pass on the morning of the 23rd, intending to harass Malanyu. The situation is dangerous because Malanyu is only eight li away from Malan Pass. After receiving the report, the county government immediately notified all parties to request assistance. The militia of the second district of Jixian County have deployed at Weiziyu Xiaoxifengkou. The militia of the eighth district have also fully mobilized. The Pinggu County militia have also been dispatched to defend. The special police unit of Zhang Qingyu was ordered by the Commissioner's Office to send a company to station at Mashen Bridge to prevent the bandits from fleeing. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Tianjin) The 1,200 bandits led by Li Laobao who infiltrated the Great Wall at Hongshankou were besieged by the Baoan Team of Zhang Qingyu and the militia at Hanerzhuang on the 22nd. The bandits were suppressed. More than 50 bandits were captured, and the remaining bandits fled outside Hongshankou. The Baoan Team has been demobilized. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

The Executive Yuan Extends Sympathy to Disaster Victims and Orders Provinces to Investigate Disaster Conditions and Exempt Taxes 7

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan has ordered the provinces in disaster areas to ascertain the severity of the disasters in their respective counties, request full or partial exemption from this year's land taxes and various surcharges, and suspend all non-urgent matters to show sympathy for the suffering people of Jiangsu. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

President Wang to Arrive at the Yuan Tomorrow to Assume Duties; Received Wang Shijie and Others Yesterday 8

(Nanchang) Wang Zhaoming, President of the Executive Yuan and concurrently Minister of Foreign Affairs, is scheduled to arrive at the Yuan on the 26th to assume his duties. Wang, as concurrent Foreign Minister, has resumed his duties, and there are important official documents from the ministry. All documents were sent to Wang's residence at the Iron Ministry's No. 1 official residence on the 24th, and Wang personally reviewed them. President Wang also received Fan Hansheng, the Consul-General stationed in Korea, at his official residence in the Iron Ministry and inquired about everything. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Nanjing) President Wang is scheduled to arrive at the Executive Yuan on the morning of the 26th to assume his duties and will attend the Executive Yuan's memorial week to report on the process of withdrawing his resignation. After the memorial week, he will go to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to handle official business. Vice Minister Xu Mo will be relieved of his responsibility as acting minister on the 26th. Wang's illness has recovered eight or nine tenths, but his physical strength and spirit are slightly worse than before. He does not plan to go to Shanghai recently. If necessary, he may invite Dr. Noel to come to Nanjing for treatment. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Nanjing) President Wang telegraphed to resume his duties on the 23rd. On the morning of the 24th, he went from his private residence in the mausoleum to the official residence of the Iron Ministry. He successively received Wang Shijie, Peng Xuepei, and Fan Hansheng, the Consul-General of Korea. Wang is scheduled to arrive at the Yuan on the 26th to assume his duties and will attend the memorial week at the Executive Yuan to report. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Suma Visits Tang Youren 9

(Nanjing) Suma, the Japanese Consul-General stationed in Nanjing, visited Tang Youren, the Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 10:30 on the morning of the 24th to discuss important matters. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Qin Dechun and Xiao Zhenying to be Appointed to New Positions Soon 10

(Beiping) Qin Dechun and Xiao Zhenying will go to Tianjin by the same train tonight to visit Song and report. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Beiping) Qin Dechun will go to Tianjin tonight to visit Song for instructions. The Central Government relies on him very much. It is heard that the announcement of his new position will be made soon. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Beiping) Qin Dechun arrived in Beiping last night. After attending Tada Hayao's tea party this afternoon, he is scheduled to return to Tianjin tonight to visit Song and report. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan will come to Beiping soon. Qin Dechun will return to Chahar to take charge of the government after Song's new position is announced. Xiao Zhenying will make a trip to Nanjing within days. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

He Yingqin Has No Preparations to Return North Yet 11

(Nanjing) Although He Yingqin, the Acting Chairman of the Beiping Military Branch, has recovered from his liver disease, he is very busy with ministry affairs and is urgently awaiting their handling. Recently, he has no intention of leaving Nanjing to return north, and there are no preparations for returning north in his residence in Nanjing. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Tada Visits Important Military and Political Figures in Beiping and Holds a Tea Party for a Social Gathering 12

(Beiping) Tada Hayao, the commander of the Japanese army in Tianjin, accompanied by his staff and Takahashi, the military attache of the Japanese Embassy, visited Wang Kemin at the Political Reorganization Committee this morning to exchange greetings on his arrival. He then visited Bao Wenyou, the director of the office at the Military Branch, and finally visited Yuan Liang, the mayor of the city government. After a brief tour, he returned to the Japanese Consulate. At 2:00 p.m., he received greetings from various Chinese and foreign parties. At 5:00 p.m., he held a tea party at the Japanese Embassy to entertain Chinese and foreign officials. The Chinese military and political authorities' invitation tonight was declined by Tada due to time constraints. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Wang Kemin Went to Nanjing Yesterday in Response to Wang's Summons 13

(Beiping) Wang Kemin left Beiping for Nanjing this evening in response to Wang's telegram summons. Those who saw him off at the station included Shang Zhen, Yuan Liang, Yu Jin, Yin Rukeng, and Wang Shuchang, and several dozens of others. The fourth team of the security force was on guard at the station. Wang was accompanied by his wife, daughter, and secretary Min Dongli. According to Wang, this trip was in response to Wang's telegram summons. The round trip is scheduled for one week. It is undecided whether he will transfer to Mogan Mountain. The Political Reorganization Committee decided to postpone the meeting to the beginning of next month. The date will be determined after he returns to Beiping. He Yingqin's return north has been reported to me, but the date is not yet determined. Rumors that there are changes in the organization of the Political Reorganization Committee are inaccurate. The suspects arrested in the Liu Zuo Zhou case have been interrogated separately, and we are working hard to arrest the real murderers. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Tianjin) He Qigong arrived in Tianjin from Beiping at 5:00 p.m. on the 24th and is scheduled to go south on the same train with Wang Kemin tonight. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Hebei Provincial Government and Others Host Tianjin Reporters 14

(Tianjin) The Hebei Provincial Government and the Tianjin-Gugu Garrison Headquarters hosted reporters at the National Hotel in the French Concession of the city at 6:30 p.m. on the 24th. More than 70 Chinese and foreign reporters attended. Chairman Shang Zhen had already gone to Beiping and Chen Wenhong, the director of the Garrison Headquarters, and the staff of the provincial government stationed in Tianjin were in charge of the reception. Zhuang Yuling, the secretary of the provincial government, delivered a speech on behalf of the provincial government. Yamauchi Reiro, a reporter from the Japanese News Agency, and Chinese reporter Li Ran delivered thank-you speeches. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Yin Rugeng Talks About the Slightly Suppressed Bandit Atmosphere in the War Zone; Visited Wang Kemin Yesterday and Reported 15

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng arrived in Beiping from Tangshan by train last night. He visited Shang this morning but did not meet him. He then went to the Political Reorganization Committee to visit Wang Kemin and report. Yin said that he had not heard anything about the transfer of the magistrate of Jixian County. The special police in the war zone will be renamed the Hebei Security Team based on the Hebei Security Headquarters. The bandit atmosphere in the war zone is relatively calm, but there are still incidents at various passes of the Great Wall from time to time. [Unclear text in the original] .The case is still under investigation. In addition to attending Tada's tea party, I came to Beiping to visit Shang and ask for instructions on important matters. The date of my return to Tangshan is not yet determined. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Beiping) Yin Tong arrived in Beiping this morning to visit Wang Kemin and report on important matters. After attending Tada's tea party in the evening, he will return to Tianjin. According to him, the suspects arrested in the Shihe robbery case are still under strict interrogation. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

County Magistrate of Jixian Dismissed for Ineffective Arrest of Murderers in Liu Case 16

(Tianjin) According to a telegram from Baoding, Chen Huishi, the magistrate of Jixian County, was dismissed by order of the provincial government on the 23rd for ineffective arrest of murderers in the Liu Zuo Zhou case, failing to solve the case within the time limit. His position will be taken over by Wang Xinggong, the magistrate of Ji County. Shi Delin has been appointed to fill the vacancy left in Ji County. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Beiping) According to a letter from Tangshan, more than 200 suspects have been arrested in the Liu Zuo Zhou assassination case. Zhang Weixiang, the secretary-general of the headquarters, went to Yuguan on official business a few days ago and was detained by the Japanese side. He is now being held in the Yuguan consulate. According to the Japanese side, Zhang is a major suspect, so he was detained and is now under strict interrogation. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

He Jian Visits Zhang Xueliang and Reports on Hunan's Military and Political Affairs 17

(Hankou) He Jian visited Zhang Xueliang on the 24th to report on Hunan's military and political affairs and visited He Chengjun and others to discuss the suppression of the remaining bandits. He is scheduled to return to Hunan tonight. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Hankou) He Jian will return to Hunan on the evening of the 24th. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Hankou Chamber of Commerce Considers Issuing Financial Bonds 18

(Hankou) The Hankou Industry Association has suggested to the Chamber of Commerce to request the central government to emulate the precedent of providing financial relief to Shanghai by issuing 20 million yuan in financial bonds, tasking banks with providing small loans to industry, commerce, and Qianzhuang, to maintain the Hankou market. The Chamber of Commerce is carefully considering this. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Commercial Depression: Tianjin's Tax Revenue Falls Short 19

(Tianjin) Due to the depression of industry and commerce in Tianjin, with numerous bankruptcies, the city's tax revenue is directly affected and reduced. The city's budget for the 24th year is planned to be reduced to 5 million yuan for the whole year, but the estimated income is only 4 million yuan, with a shortfall of more than 1 million yuan. It has not been completed so far. The city's overall business tax survey for the 24th year has also become a problem due to the increase in tax rates and has not yet started. The city's total revenue in July was only 200,000 yuan, a decrease of more than 150,000 yuan. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Typhoon to Make Landfall in Fujian Province 20

(Nanjing) According to the Central Meteorological Observatory, the typhoon reached the Taiwan Strait on the afternoon of the 24th and is still moving northwest at a slow speed. It will make landfall in Xiamen and Fuzhou on the evening of the 24th. The wind is not strong. The wind on the southeast coast has become stronger, and the lower reaches of the Yangtze River will also be affected on the 25th. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

(Xiamen) Xiamen has been affected by the Taiwan hurricane since the 23rd, with wind. It strengthened on the morning of the 24th and became stronger at noon. The wind weakened in the evening. The sky cleared and the temperature rose to 94 degrees, an increase of seven or eight degrees compared to the previous two days. It is sultry and there is no rain. Coastal ships near Quanzhou are still operating on the 24th because the wind has not arrived. Small ships on the inland rivers of Zhangzhou and Xiamen are still operating. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Medical Association to Establish Two Committees Soon 21

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Education and the Department of Health have agreed on the list of 11 members each for the Nurse and Midwife Specialized Committees of the Ministry of Education's Medical Association. The announcement will be made soon, and the two committees will be established. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Request to Issue Shipping Bonds: The Ministry Approves That It Cannot Be Done 22

(Nanjing) The Shanghai Shipping Industry Association has submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications to consult the Ministry of Finance to issue 10 million yuan of shipping bonds in advance. The Ministry of Communications issued an approval on the 24th, stating that after consulting the Ministry of Finance, it was found that the association had already telegraphed the Ministry of Communications about this case. When the association requested the issuance of 10 million yuan of shipping bonds, it was because the funds could not be transferred, and it was not convenient to discuss the issuance at that time. They should find their own ways to raise funds for relief. Now, the national treasury is even more strained than before. The request is still impossible to grant, and a telegram has been sent in response. With this approval, it is hereby notified that the matter has been reviewed. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Teichman to Return to His Country Via Xinjiang 23

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic sources, Sir Eric Teichman, Counselor of the British Embassy in China, plans to return to his country in early September from Guisui along the Sui-Xin Highway via Xinjiang. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Higher Education Examination Committee to be Set Up in Nanjing and Guangzhou 24

(Nanjing) The Higher Education Examination Committee this year will only be set up in Nanjing and Guangzhou. An office will be set up in Beiping and Shaanxi, each under the jurisdiction of the First Examination Committee in Nanjing. All candidates taking the exam in Beiping and Shaanxi must go to Nanjing for the final exam after passing the first or second exam. It is reported that the number of registration forms has reached [unclear number] at the Higher Education Examination registration office, and it is expected that the number of provinces taking the exam this year will be greater than in previous years. [Unclear text in the original]

(Special dispatch on the 24th)

Minor Private Salt Cases to be Punished According to the Regulations Promulgated by the Ministry 25

(Nanjing) The government previously formulated and promulgated the Law on Punishing Crimes Related to Private Salt. The Ministry of Finance believes that the law can only be applied to punish serious private salt cases. For minor cases, it is stipulated that they should be handled in accordance with the Regulations on Punishing Minor Private Salt Cases promulgated by the Ministry. It has specially consulted the Ministry of Justice and requested that all courts be notified not to accept minor private salt cases. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Yunnan Province Stamps to Implement National Currency Calculation Method 26

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications has decided to implement the national currency calculation method for Yunnan Province stamps, abolish the limited use of old stamps, and has consulted the Yunnan Provincial Government to assist in the implementation to ensure the postal service and benefit national operations. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

A Thousand-Mile Horse Arrived in Nanjing Yesterday 27

(Nanjing) It was reported that Han Fuqu gave a thousand-mile horse to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. It was transported to Nanjing from Jinan on the 23rd. According to the Third Army Office, the horse arrived in Nanjing on the 24th and was given by Han to Counselor Yang Jie, not to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Simple Life Insurance to be Included in Textbooks 28

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications believes that in order to popularize simple life insurance handled by the post office throughout the country, in addition to adopting various forms of publicity, it should also follow the example of other countries and include the insurance system in elementary school textbooks as teaching material to achieve popularization. It has recently consulted the Ministry of Education to review and implement this. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

US Vice President to Visit the Philippines This Autumn 29

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic sources, US Vice President Garner and more than 40 members of the Senate and House of Representatives are scheduled to visit the Philippines this autumn to attend the inauguration ceremony of the first President of the Philippines. The voyage will pass through Japan and Shanghai. Whether they will travel in China or not, the relevant parties have not yet received notification. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission Staff Donate Salaries to Help Disaster Relief 30

(Nanjing) Considering the extraordinarily severe floods in the Yangtze and Yellow Rivers this year, the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission passed its 103rd Standing Committee meeting on the 24th, and the commission's colleagues will donate 5% of their salaries and official expenses to help disaster relief. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Kong Xiangxi Writes an Article to Commemorate Confucius' Birthday 31

(Nanjing) Since Confucius' birthday is approaching, Kong Xiangxi has written an article explaining Confucius' daily life and the meaning of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, with an attached table for explanation. It will be sent to various newspapers for publication soon. The Confucius Temple in Yuncheng, Shanxi, is currently being renovated by the Hedong Salt Transport Commissioner, and a library is being built as an attachment. It has been reported to the central government for record. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

The Executive Yuan Orders the Appointment of Committee Members to Manage Disaster Relief Funds in Hubei 32

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan has ordered the appointment of Jia Shiyi, Meng Guangpeng, and others as members of the Hubei Province Disaster Relief Reserve Fund Management Committee, and has designated Jia Shiyi as the chairman of the committee. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

(Hankou) The Flood Relief Headquarters telegraphed all health teams to carry out epidemic prevention measures and implement disinfection. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Department of Health to Handle Registration of Prepared Medicines 33

(Nanjing) The Department of Health will start handling the general registration of prepared medicines nationwide from today until December 31st of this year. During this period, the inspection fee for each type of medicine will be 15 yuan, the certificate fee will be 2 yuan, and the stamp duty will be 1 yuan. The Executive Yuan has approved the record and notified all medical institutions nationwide to comply. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Scheduled Burial of Liao Zhongkai 34

(Nanjing) After the remains of martyr Liao Zhongkai were moved to Nanjing, the central government appointed Chen Shuren as the preparation director to select a burial site. The Tianbao City cemetery has been selected, and the burial will be held on September 1st. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Current Commentary

Autumn Term Begins 35

— Bing

Autumn has arrived, and the summer vacation is over. Schools at all levels will soon reopen their classrooms, filled with the sound of students chanting. While this is a common occurrence, it coincides with a particularly unusual time. There is something I wish to say to all students across the nation.

During this summer vacation, our people have suffered profound and deep pain. Everyone remains silent, seemingly unaware. Yet, they understand each other in their hearts, etched in their minds. Their anxiety and anger far outweigh the fear of facing imminent death. Furthermore, floods have inundated rivers, turning cities into swamps. Lives are lost to the waves, and property is utterly destroyed. Cries of sorrow echo everywhere, and newspapers overflow with urgent appeals for help. Human actions and natural disasters combine to inflict suffering, making any descriptive terms of misery and pain insufficient to depict the current situation of our people. In such times, students should behave differently from those living in peaceful and stable eras.

To say that all responsibilities of a nation belong solely to students is far from reasonable and not well-considered. However, in our country, being able to have one's name on the school roll and study in lecture halls is not something everyone can achieve. From a worldly perspective, it is considered a blessing. From a realistic point of view, it is, in fact, receiving the benevolence of the masses. These masses are not affluent; rather, they are draining their meager resources to support students. Students receiving this touching and pitiable benevolence should establish firm aspirations. They should aim to shoulder a greater share of responsibility and contribute a larger portion of their strength in the future. They should repay the masses who have nurtured them, transform this unusual time, and guide the nation onto a path of stability and prosperity. If even now they fail to consider this and instead spend their days in frivolous pleasure, wasting time in idleness, they will be deeply indebted to the masses, and their guilt will be impossible to redeem. As the school term begins, I urge all students to think about this again and again.

Merely stating ambitions is like an empty promise. It is necessary to cultivate practical abilities, upon which ambitions can be grounded. The ways to cultivate practical abilities are numerous, but let me mention the essentials.

History is the comprehensive record of past stumbles. Ignorance of the past makes it impossible to recognize the path forward. How then can one take action? Now, people view us as a dependency, using sweet words and threats in concert, attempting to erase recent history. This aims to make our people, from the present generation to our descendants, gradually forget these blood-stained pages. They believe this is a good plan. But should we simply obey their wishes? I urge you, students, to observe this. From now on, you should dedicate yourselves to studying history, especially recent history. Experts have statistically found that, in general, students are remarkably ignorant of history. This is a serious problem that urgently needs correction.

Economics is the foundation of life. In today's interconnected world, the flow of resources is intimately linked. The authorities of a country are like the management of a large corporation, and without the ability to maneuver and strategize, everything comes down to shrewd calculations and profitable gains. If we are ignorant of the current state of the economy, we will not know where our lives can be secured. Why are hundreds of industries declining? Who is to blame for the bankruptcy of rural villages? We must investigate the causes and examine the structures to understand that if our people truly wish to survive, there is a path we must follow. Crying out to overthrow imperialism may be seen as extreme. But practically speaking, mere shouting accomplishes nothing. Without shouting, but with a practical and grounded approach, there may be a chance of success. I urge you, students, to understand this. From now on, dedicate yourselves to studying economics, with the survival of our people as your starting point. Do not think that this subject is dry and dull, less palatable than poetry and novels, and therefore abandon it.

The various fields of science are the methods of sustaining life. They primarily deal with the myriad phenomena of the world, not just the study of language and writing. Only for the convenience of transmission and dissemination are they categorized and written in books. Those who study should focus on the objects themselves, so that every piece of knowledge gained is useful in their lives. However, in our country, the common practice is to equate learning with reading, and reading is seen as merely a woman's adornment, a decoration for life. Consequently, those who study science exhaust their minds on books, without verifying their knowledge through observation of the world. They can recite the entire book of botany but do not understand the physiology of weeds and crops. They study physics for years but forget to apply it to daily life. The names of scientific education and vocational education have been promoted for a long time, but there have been no visible results. Although there are many reasons for this, the wrong approach to studying science from the start is a major cause. I urge you, students, to understand this. From now on, focus on the objects themselves, with books as supplementary aids. Do not simply read, but seek practical knowledge. Some new educators advocate for "learning by doing," which is something that should be followed.

To elaborate further would exceed the limits of space. In short, learning for the sake of learning is the extravagant talk of boastful scholars, with no relevance to reality. Today, all our learning must be purposeful. What is that purpose? It is to cultivate practical abilities through learning, to establish firm ambitions to shoulder great responsibilities. As the school term begins, I urge you, students, to recognize this seriously.

Berlin Museum Accepts Famous Chinese Paintings 36

The Chinese government therefore decided to donate these sixteen famous paintings to the German Museum. The museum has specially created a section to display these paintings, indicating Germany's recognition of China's creative achievements. Minister Rust, on behalf of the German government, expressed his gratitude and stated that the German people have always deeply respected China's long history and culture. Page 9

Mussolini Explains the Purpose of the Expedition: To Protect Rights and Promote Civilization; All Existing Treaties Remain in Effect 38

(Rome) In high spirits, Prime Minister Mussolini declared today that the solution to the Abyssinian problem must be decisive and thorough. In order to avoid conflict, we have tried to seek understanding with Abyssinia. Therefore, we signed the Italian-Abyssinian Treaty of Friendship in 1928. However, Abyssinia has consistently disregarded the treaty. I have decided to send troops to Eritrea and Somalia as a precautionary measure. I do not hate any nation, but I insist that Italy's rights must be respected.

Asked whether Italy's policy would jeopardize European security and the Anglo-French-Italian understanding established at the Stresa Conference, Mussolini replied that he did not believe Italy's actions in Abyssinia would affect Italy's full support for European cooperation policy, as the actions in Africa were purely local in nature. What could jeopardize the results of the Stresa Conference and European security is the attitude of those who disregard Italy's needs for security and development, those who exaggerate the consequences of Italy's actions to create alarm. Our actions in Abyssinia are the same as those of other colonial countries in Asia and Africa. Mussolini then recounted the history of aggression by various countries, such as the British bombing of Alexandria in 1882 and the American occupation of West Indian and Mexican territories, which were too numerous to list.

Asked how Italy would handle the situation if the League of Nations' mediation failed and whether it would withdraw from the League of Nations, Mussolini replied that Italy would definitely pursue its claims. It is acceptable to cooperate with the League of Nations, but it is also acceptable not to cooperate with the League of Nations. I do not believe that safeguarding the security of a country can be said to violate the League of Nations Covenant.

Regarding how to avoid war and the future of the League of Nations, Mussolini earnestly stated that the progress of a country like Italy cannot be stopped by a static view of life. This static view of life is the greatest factor threatening world peace. If the League of Nations hopes to continue to exist, it must understand that Articles 19 and 22 of its Covenant express this threat. The League of Nations Covenant is part of the Treaty of Versailles, Article 282 of which confirmed the provisions of the 1888 Convention, which provides for free passage through the Suez Canal in both peacetime and wartime.

Asked whether Italy would search neutral ships in wartime, Mussolini replied that Italy would always strictly abide by international law.

Asked whether Britain's attitude on this matter was entirely driven by justice, Mussolini replied that in the treaties of 1891 and 1894, Britain recognized all of Abyssinia's territory and Italy's sphere of influence. These treaties are still in effect. Britain's interests in the Nile are also specifically recognized. Britain's interests in Abyssinia are therefore fully guaranteed. The lack of understanding of Italy's legitimate demands in some quarters in Britain seems inconsistent with the requirement to protect British rights in Africa.

Asked how to restore the lost power of the white race, Mussolini replied that he had long drawn the world's attention to the decline in the fertility of Westerners. The world should know how the Fascist government is increasing and improving the population. If the decline in the fertility of Western people is followed by the abandonment of the obligation to promote civilization among the closed-minded nations, the future will be truly unthinkable. Mussolini was wearing civilian clothes when he made this statement. (National News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

London Officials Refute Mussolini's Remarks: The League of Nations Covenant Must Be Respected 39

(London) London officials believe that Prime Minister Mussolini's declaration yesterday, stating that the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia had begun forty years ago, is not entirely accurate. The reason is that Abyssinia's accession to the League of Nations was initiated by Italy to the League of Nations. At that time, in 1923, Italy made no mention of any dispute. In his declaration, the Prime Minister also stated that Italy's actions, whether the League of Nations agrees or opposes, will continue. This not only violates the League of Nations Covenant but also contradicts the 1928 Italian-Abyssinian Arbitration Agreement. In addition, the Kellogg-Briand Pact and the 1930 Treaty all guaranteed Abyssinia's territorial integrity, which cannot be simply dismissed. Moreover, regarding the attitude of the small countries in the League of Nations, these countries regard the League of Nations as their support. Now that a conflict has occurred between Italy and Abyssinia, although Italy claims it is a local dispute, it will undermine the authority of the League of Nations, which is related to the safety of these small countries. Therefore, these countries cannot ignore it. According to recent news, the countries of the Little Entente, the three Scandinavian countries, and Turkey all believe that the League of Nations Covenant must be respected, which can be seen. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Mediterranean Countries Conduct Preparations Separately; British Fleet to Depart for Patrol at the End of the Month; Defenses Increased in the Gibraltar Area 40

(London) As the situation between Italy and Abyssinia intensifies, all major powers related to the Mediterranean are taking precautionary measures to prevent unexpected incidents and protect their national interests. The matter is confidential, so outsiders have little way of knowing the details of their actions. Paris is extremely secretive, but it is reported that France is now seeking to increase its naval strength in its Mediterranean ports. According to news from Palma, Spain, the Spanish government has sent two teams of field artillery to Ibiza, the westernmost island, and will deploy five battalions of infantry to the Balearic Islands. It is reported that a British ship recently unloaded two 15-inch caliber cannons at the port of Mahon on the west coast of Minorca, Spain, for the newly built forts there. Although officials in British Gibraltar have not formally announced the strength of the Mediterranean Fleet, the movements of warships are known as follows: (1) The Second Destroyer Flotilla sailed from Malta yesterday. (2) The aircraft carrier HMS Glorious is scheduled to arrive in Gibraltar tomorrow and will stay there for half a month. (3) Two destroyers, HMS Searcher and HMS Wessex, will arrive in Gibraltar shortly. Today, officials in Malta denied reports of an increase in the strength of the British Mediterranean Fleet. However, officials announced a few days ago that the old battleship HMS Royal Sovereign would be replaced by the stronger battleship HMS Barham. The patrol schedule of the British Mediterranean Fleet has now also been confirmed. The ships will depart on August 29, but will not go to the Adriatic ports. The First Cruiser Squadron, the Third Cruiser Squadron, two battleships, and one aircraft carrier will go to Alexandria. Several other warships will go to other ports. The First Destroyer Flotilla, the First Submarine Squadron, and one battleship will remain in Malta until the end of September. It is rumored in Gibraltar today that several U.S. warships will arrive there shortly, but the U.S. Consulate in Gibraltar has not received such news. At the same time, the number of Spanish troops arriving in the area near Gibraltar is increasing daily. According to a dispatch from Athens, the Italian authorities have ordered all residents of the Dodecanese Islands in the Aegean Sea to evacuate so that the islands can be converted into a military hospital base, as the climate is good and there are many forests, which are very suitable. (Reuters dispatch, 24th)

Suez Canal Busy with Italian Ships Transporting Troops; Mussolini's Two Sons and Son-in-Law Enlist in the Army 41

(London) The Daily Telegraph reported that Prime Minister Mussolini's war plan is underway, so the Suez Canal is unusually busy today. An Italian destroyer squadron arrived in Port Said and then passed through the canal into the Red Sea. Following them were two ships full of war supplies and coal for the Italian army in Africa. Soon after, another Italian transport ship carrying 1,200 soldiers and another ship carrying 200 people passed through the canal and headed to Massawa in Eritrea, where the Italian military base is located. At the same time, an Italian ship carrying sixty sick soldiers from Eritrea sailed in the opposite direction, as the heat there is severe and many Italian soldiers have died from illness. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

Cairo Italian ship traffic through the Suez Canal increased suddenly today. Five ships, including a destroyer, headed south. Another ship, carrying sick soldiers from Eritrea, headed back to Italy. Of the four southbound ships, two were carrying troops, one carrying 1,200 officers and men, and the other carrying 200. The other two ships were carrying military supplies. (National News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Rome) Mussolini's two sons and son-in-law are scheduled to leave Naples today for service in East Africa. The son-in-law is Count Ciano, the former Italian ambassador to China, who is now the Minister of Press and Propaganda. All three are officers in the Italian Air Force. (Reuters dispatch, 24th)

Naples A steamship carrying 40 officers, 400 Blackshirts, and 100 gendarmes set sail at 5 p.m. for East Africa. Another steamship, carrying 124 officers and 3,684 party soldiers, is also ready to depart. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

(Rome) Eight thousand members of the Fascist Party army are scheduled to depart from the port of Naples tomorrow for Italian territories in East Africa. In addition, another 16,000 party soldiers will also travel to East Africa on 18 ships. The Air Force needs 4,600 more personnel to serve in East Africa. After an announcement, more than 16,000 people have applied so far. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

(Rome) The famous tropical disease expert Sir Aldo Castellani has been hired by the Italian government as the chief health advisor to the civilians and soldiers in the Italian colonies in Africa. Sir Castellani is the uncle of Sir Miles Lampson, the former British ambassador to China and current British High Commissioner in Egypt. He is 58 years old and is known worldwide for his research on tropical diseases. He has written several books on such diseases and often publishes scientific papers in various magazines. He served in the Italian Royal Medical Corps during the European War. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

Britain's Special Position in Egypt and Sudan Will Change Due to the War 42

Cairo The Italo-Abyssinian dispute will change Britain's special position in Egypt and Sudan. People here now anticipate two possibilities: (1) If Britain and Italy clash, Egypt's position vis-à-vis Britain will change. (2) British troops may occupy the Lake Tana area with or without Egyptian troops, or they may do so alone. The impression here that Britain will take anti-Italian action has been largely dispelled since receiving yesterday's London telegram. However, the general opinion is that Britain cannot allow Italy to extend its power to the Nile waters. If no agreement is reached in advance, British troops will occupy the Lake Tana area before Italian troops arrive. As for the Suez Canal, people here do not believe that closing the canal is within the scope of practical politics, nor can it be achieved through the League of Nations. However, if it is not done by the League of Nations, but by a single country such as Britain, it would be tantamount to a declaration of war. At the same time, rumors are circulating that a British brigade will be stationed at the Suez Canal, which has not been stationed by troops until now. The news that General Spinks, the commander-in-chief of the Egyptian army, was recalled from vacation is attracting widespread attention. Rumors of an increase in British troops stationed in Egypt are rife, but so far no British troops have been seen arriving. At the same time, special training for reconnaissance is being conducted by air force squadrons in the Nile River basin and the Egyptian desert. Sir Miles Lampson, the British High Commissioner in Egypt, recently inspected the military sites, reminding people of recent events. British troops have been engaged in desert training in the last five years, so it is not difficult for British troops to cross the Abyssinian border and advance to Lake Tana. Influential Egyptians are now disgusted with Italy's expansion in Africa. They see Italy as a dangerous neighbor and see the Anglo-Egyptian alliance as not being in the spirit of mutual benefit. It is reported that plans to protect the safety of British nationals in Abyssinia and their eventual withdrawal will also be applied to Egyptian nationals in Abyssinia. This is enough to prove the friendship between Britain and Egypt. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

(Rome) A magazine called "October" published here today an article discussing the Anglo-Italian war. The content shows that it is prepared for any armed intervention or attempt to impose sanctions by any country. The article first compares the military positions of the two countries in the Mediterranean, and then states that Britain's blockade of the Suez Canal is the fuse for a war between Britain and Italy. It also states that if a war breaks out between Britain and Italy, the size of the two countries' navies will be relegated to secondary importance, while the air force will occupy the primary position. It is also said that in terms of Italy's naval strength in the western and central Mediterranean, it is very easy to block the sea route between Sicily and North Africa, and there is enough power to maintain the transportation of the Strait of Messina for its own use. It is then stated that the Strait of Gibraltar and the naval base of Malta under British control can easily be destroyed by the air force. Therefore, Italy's situation in the Mediterranean, in terms of air warfare, is in an extremely advantageous position. Finally, the report claims that Italy is able to defeat any pressure in the Mediterranean war and will soon prove it in practice. (National News Agency dispatch, 24th)

U.S. House of Representatives Passes Neutrality Act; Compromise Acceptable to the President 43

(Washington) The House of Representatives today passed the U.S. Neutrality Act, which stipulates that the President must declare a ban on the shipment of munitions to belligerent countries when war breaks out in other countries. The purpose of this act is to protect the United States' neutrality in the event of a European war. The main points are the same as those passed by the Senate, so it is expected that the Senate will accept the amendments proposed by the House of Representatives. Although this mandatory or non-discretionary ban will expire at the end of February 1936, a permanent licensing system for the manufacture and export of munitions under the supervision of cabinet commissioners will be established. In addition to banning the shipment of munitions to belligerent countries, this act also prohibits U.S. citizens from traveling on belligerent ships and does not allow belligerent warships to use U.S. ports. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

(Washington) A bill to maintain U.S. neutrality in wartime, after being passed by the Senate, was immediately sent to the House of Representatives for discussion, where it was rejected and an amendment was passed advocating that the United States should ban the shipment of munitions to belligerent countries, but its effect is limited to February 29, 1936. As a compromise, this compromise bill will be discussed by the Senate for one hour today. This compromise bill is in line with President Roosevelt's wishes. The President believes that with Congress adjourning soon, there is not enough time to establish a definitive bill, so he requested the passage of a temporary bill. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

(Washington) Democratic Senator Homer Bone, who is in London, reportedly stated in England that the United States would not be able to remain neutral in the next war. It is also reported that he met with British Foreign Secretary Hoare and Labour Party leader Lansbury. People in the Senate are very upset about this behavior by Bone. Although Bone claims his trip to England is personal, it is reported that he met with President Roosevelt and Secretary of State Hull before going to Europe. Many Republicans say Bone's actions are similar to those of Colonel House in the past. Colonel House was a close friend of President Wilson who visited European governments in 1914, 1915, and 1916, before the United States joined the European War. Senators who advocate U.S. isolationism strongly disapprove of Bone's actions, saying that his activities will plunge the United States into the European vortex. (Reuters dispatch, 24th)

Meningitis Rampant in Tokyo; High Mortality Rate from Sleeping Sickness 62

(Nanjing) Epidemic meningitis has spread to Tokyo. The Metropolitan Police Department's disease prevention division has mobilized all its staff to prevent the disease. According to the division's investigation, from January to the end of July this year, a total of twelve people in Tokyo contracted the disease, and all died. From August 1st to 21st, another five people contracted the disease, and all died. On the 22nd, three new cases occurred, one of whom died. The disease prevention division is finding it difficult to prevent the disease due to its unknown source. (24th Japan United Press Telegram)

(Tokyo) Meningitis is increasingly rampant in Tokyo. As of the 24th, there have been fifty-one new cases and twenty deaths. (24th Japan United Press Telegram)

(Tokyo) The number of people suffering from sleeping sickness is gradually increasing nationwide, and the mortality rate is also rising. Health authorities are greatly alarmed. It is reported that there are already seventy-five cases in Tokyo alone, with nearly half proving fatal. The total number of patients nationwide has exceeded five hundred. An investigation shows that in 1924, there were 6,125 cases, which decreased to 1,946 in 1929. There were no cases last year, but the disease has re-emerged this year, possibly due to the revival of dormant viruses after the weather cooled. (24th Reuters Telegram)
